\"text\": \"# Kafka Configuration Annotation Pattern Discovery\\n\\nIn Apache Kafka, the configuration management system uses the @ConfigDef and @ConfigKey pattern (though these are classes rather than Java annotations) to provide a declarative way to define and document configuration options. This pattern is extensively used throughout the kafka repository.\\n\\n## Key Components\\n\\n### Core Framework (clients module)\\n\\n**ConfigDef** (`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/ConfigDef.java`) is the main class that defines configuration schemas. It contains a nested class **ConfigKey** that represents individual configuration parameters with properties like name, type, default value, validator, importance, documentation, group, and display information.\\n\\n**AbstractConfig** (`clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/config/AbstractConfig.java`) is the base class that all concrete configuration classes extend. It provides methods for parsing and accessing configuration values using a ConfigDef schema.\\n\\n### Configuration Classes Using the Pattern\\n\\nThe ConfigDef/ConfigKey pattern is used extensively throughout Kafka:\\n\\n**Client Configurations:**\\n- `ConsumerConfig` - Kafka consumer configuration options\\n- `ProducerConfig` - Kafka producer configuration options\\n- `AdminClientConfig` - Admin client configuration with main method generating HTML documentation\\n\\n**Streams Configurations:**\\n- `StreamsConfig` - Kafka Streams configuration options with toHtml() documentation generator\\n- `TopologyConfig` - Topology-specific configuration options\\n\\n**Connect Configurations:**\\n- `ConnectorConfig` - Base configuration for all connectors\\n- `SinkConnectorConfig` - Sink connector configuration with main method\\n- `SourceConnectorConfig` - Source connector configuration with main method\\n- `WorkerConfig` - Connect worker configuration\\n- `TaskConfig` - Task configuration\\n- `ConverterConfig` - Base converter configuration\\n- `JsonConverterConfig` - JSON converter configuration\\n- `StringConverterConfig` - String converter configuration\\n- `RestServerConfig` - REST server configuration\\n- `DistributedConfig` - Distributed Connect configuration with main method\\n- `MirrorConnectorConfig` - Mirror connector base configuration with main method\\n- `MirrorSourceConfig` - Mirror source connector configuration with main method\\n- `MirrorHeartbeatConfig` - Mirror heartbeat configuration with main method\\n- `MirrorCheckpointConfig` - Mirror checkpoint configuration with main method\\n- `MirrorClientConfig` - Mirror client configuration\\n\\n**Server/Broker Configurations:**\\n- `KafkaConfig` (Scala) - Broker configuration with main method generating HTML documentation\\n- `LogConfig` - Topic/log configuration with main method\\n- `GroupConfig` - Group coordinator configuration with main method\\n- `RemoteLogManagerConfig` - Remote log manager configuration with main method\\n- `TopicBasedRemoteLogMetadataManagerConfig` - Remote log metadata manager configuration with main method\\n- `ClientMetricsConfigs` - Client metrics configuration\\n\\n**Supporting Configuration Classes:**\\n- `TopicConfig` - Topic-level configuration constants\\n- `SslConfigs` - SSL/TLS configuration constants\\n- `SaslConfigs` - SASL configuration constants\\n- `SecurityConfig` - Security configuration\\n- `KRaftConfigs` - KRaft mode configuration\\n- `QuotaConfig` - Quota configuration\\n\\n### Documentation Generation Chain\\n\\nThe ConfigDef class provides a `toHtml()` method that generates HTML documentation from the configuration schema. Configuration classes implement a `main()` method that uses this functionality to generate documentation:\\n\\n- **PredicateDoc** - Generates HTML documentation for predicates\\n- **TransformationDoc** - Generates HTML documentation for transformations\\n\\nMany configuration classes have `main()` methods that call `configDef().toHtml()` to generate documentation. These are invoked by Gradle build tasks (seen in build.gradle):\\n- `genKafkaConfigDocs` - generates kafka_config.html\\n- `genTopicConfigDocs` - generates topic_config.html\\n- `genGroupConfigDocs` - generates group_config.html\\n\\n### REST API Layer\\n\\nFor Connect REST APIs, configuration information is exposed through:\\n- `ConfigInfo` - Contains configuration definition and values\\n- `ConfigKeyInfo` - Represents configuration key metadata used in REST responses\\n\\n### Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n**AbstractHerder** (`connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/AbstractHerder.java`) contains the `convertConfigKey()` method that transforms ConfigKey objects into ConfigKeyInfo for REST API responses.\\n\\n**KafkaConfigSchema** (`metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/KafkaConfigSchema.java`) provides schema validation utilities that work with ConfigDef objects.\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe ConfigDef/ConfigKey pattern provides a unified, declarative approach to configuration management throughout Apache Kafka. It enables:\\n1. Type-safe configuration definition with validation\\n2. Automatic documentation generation\\n3. Configuration schema introspection\\n4. REST API exposure of configuration metadata\\n5. Consistent handling across all components (brokers, clients, streams, connect)\\n\\nThis pattern is fundamental to Kafka's extensibility and manageability across its diverse ecosystem of components.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":8,"cache_creation_input_tokens":6586,"cache_read_input_tokens":105267,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":6586},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"0094ce40-6a47-4cde-a8a4-162e7f87f0f7","uuid":"bd3e5b7d-240a-4fa0-b284-d601df10e07d"}

Base converter configuration\\n- `JsonConverterConfig` - JSON converter configuration\\n- `StringConverterConfig` - String converter configuration\\n- `RestServerConfig` - REST server configuration\\n- `DistributedConfig` - Mirror heartbeat configuration with main method\\n- `MirrorCheckpointConfig` - Mirror checkpoint configuration with main method\\n- `MirrorClientConfig` - Mirror client configuration\\n\\n**Server/Broker Configurations:**\\n- `KafkaConfig` (Scala) - Broker configuration with main method generating HTML documentation\\n- `LogConfig` - Topic/log configuration with main method\\n- `GroupConfig` - Group coordinator configuration with main method\\n- `RemoteLogManagerConfig` - Remote log manager configuration with main method\\n- `TopicBasedRemoteLogMetadataManagerConfig` - Remote log metadata manager configuration with main method\\n- `ClientMetricsConfigs` - Client metrics configuration\\n\\n**Supporting Configuration Classes:**\\n- `TopicConfig` - Topic-level configuration constants\\n- `SslConfigs` - SSL/TLS configuration constants\\n- `SaslConfigs` - SASL configuration constants\\n- `SecurityConfig` - Security configuration\\n- `KRaftConfigs` - KRaft mode configuration\\n- `QuotaConfig` - Quota configuration\\n\\n### Documentation Generation Chain\\n\\nThe ConfigDef class provides a `toHtml()` method that generates HTML documentation from the configuration schema. Configuration classes implement a `main()` method that uses this functionality to generate documentation:\\n\\n- **PredicateDoc** - Generates HTML documentation for predicates\\n- **TransformationDoc** - Generates HTML documentation for transformations\\n\\nMany configuration classes have `main()` methods that call `configDef().toHtml()` to generate documentation. These are invoked by Gradle build tasks (seen in build.gradle):\\n- `genKafkaConfigDocs` - generates kafka_config.html\\n- `genTopicConfigDocs` - generates topic_config.html\\n- `genGroupConfigDocs` - generates group_config.html\\n\\n### REST API Layer\\n\\nFor Connect REST APIs, configuration information is exposed through:\\n- `ConfigInfo` - Contains configuration definition and values\\n- `ConfigKeyInfo` - Represents configuration key metadata used in REST responses\\n\\n### Supporting Infrastructure\\n\\n**AbstractHerder** (`connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/AbstractHerder.java`) contains the `convertConfigKey()` method that transforms ConfigKey objects into ConfigKeyInfo for REST API responses.\\n\\n**KafkaConfigSchema** (`metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/KafkaConfigSchema.java`) provides schema validation utilities that work with ConfigDef objects.\\n\\n## Summary\\n\\nThe ConfigDef/ConfigKey pattern provides a unified, declarative approach to configuration management throughout Apache Kafka. It enables:\\n1. Type-safe configuration definition with validation\\n2. Automatic documentation generation\\n3. Configuration schema introspection\\n4. REST API exposure of configuration metadata\\n5. Consistent handling across all components (brokers, clients, streams, connect)\\n\\nThis pattern is fundamental to Kafka's extensibility and manageability across its diverse ecosystem of components.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
